2:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL:式
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?stage ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002152  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575    )
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType    )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score DESC

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY | ANATOMICALENTITY_NAME | SCORE | EFO_0005135 | Stage | Gene | expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value
### GO:0005575 | ?               | ?      | ?          | ?     | ?     | ?
###
### GO:0005575 | smooth muscle cell | 0.01 | EFO_0005135 | post-juvenile | APOC1 | 0.0000000000000000

4:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(              ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575              )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description ?anatomicalentityName ?score

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY ?ANATOMICALENTITY_LABEL ?ANATOMICALENTITY ?ANATOMICALENTITYName ?EFO_0000399 ?EF0000399_LABEL ?EF0000399_DESCRIPTION ?gene ?expression ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?score
http   http://purl.org/dc/terms/label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_00

5:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 gene is expressed independently of the developmental stage, sex, strain and cell type? Provide also the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene label.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX efo: <http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/>
    PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?strain ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_label WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
		?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
		?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
		?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
		?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
		?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
		?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "life cycle" .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
		?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain . # has strain
		?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
		?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
		?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
		?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
		?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
		?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
		?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
		?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	}

### DESCRIPTION:
This query returns the anatomical entity where the APOC1 gene is expressed independently of the developmental stage, sex, strain and cell type. Provide also the developmental stage label, the developmental stage description, the anatomical entity label, the anatomical entity description, the gene see also, the gene description, the gene label.

### EXAMPLE:
?id gene:id "APOC1" .
?id genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition.
?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 .
?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
?efo_0000399 a e

6:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_label ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?gene
### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY ?ANATOMICALENTITY_NAME ?ANATOMICALENTITY ?ANATOMICALENTITY_LABEL ?ANATOMICALENTITY_DESCRIPTION ?EFO_0000399 ?SCORE ?EXPRESSION ?Gene ?gene_identifier ###
UNIPROT
Pancreas  pancreas  http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label  http://purl.org/dc/terms/description  post-juvenile  http://purl.org/dc/terms/

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon common name.

### SPARQL:etown.

### ANSWER:
Preparing query...

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575    )
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType    )
}

### DISCUSSION:
In this query we used the following approaches:

*   We used the orth:organism relation to specify that the gene is in the human organism.

*   We used the up:taxon relation to specify the taxon.

*   We used the up:commonName property to specify the common name of the taxon.

*   We used the genex:hasAnatomicalEntity relation to specify the anatomical entity.

*   We used the genex:hasAnatomicalEntity relation to specify the anatomical entity.

*   We used the genex:hasExpressionCondition relation to specify the expression condition.

*   We used the genex:hasExpressionLevel relation to specify the expression level.

*   We used the genex:hasSequenceUnit relation to specify the sequence unit.

*   We used the rdfs:label property to specify the anatomical entity name.

*   We used the rdfs:label property to specify the gene label.

*   We used the <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> property to specify the taxon common name.

	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.

	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.

13:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene_description ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity DESC ?anatomicalentityName DESC ?score DESC

19:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL:式
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has an anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has an anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has a strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(          ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575          )
} ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score DESC

### RESULT:
    Previous RDF4J version returned:
    No result found
    
    New RDF4J version returns:
    ### Anatomical entity ### Anatomical entity ### Expression level ### Gene see also ### Gene description ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label ### Gene description ### Gene see also ### Gene identifier ### Gene label

21:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0005135_label ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stage ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0005135 ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002155  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity DESC ?anatomicalentityName DESC ?score DESC

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY:  ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentityDescription ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_description ?gene

24:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_label ?gene_description ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                )
}
ORDER BY DESC(?score)

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY: ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression ?gene ?taxon ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_commonname ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_description
http://purl.org/dc/terms/Description http://purl.org/dc/terms/Description http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label http://purl.org/genex#expression http://purl.org/org/core/scientificName http://purl.uniprot.org/core/common

25:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_commonname ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_description ?taxon_scientificname ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
		?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
		?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
		?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
		?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
		?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
		?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
		?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
		?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
		?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
		?taxon a up:Taxon .
		?taxon up:commonName "human" .
		?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
		?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
		?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
		?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
		?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
		?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
		?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
		?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
		?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	}

### RESULT:
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description ?taxon_commonname ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage?

### SPARQL:ixon?

### ANSWER:
Please see the following SPARQL query:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?gene WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
		?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
		?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
		?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
		?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
		?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
		?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
		?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
		?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
		?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
		?taxon a up:Taxon .
		?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	}

### DESCRIPTION:
This query finds the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage.

### EXAMPLE:

31:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the developmental stage label.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_label ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575    )
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType    )
}
ORDER BY DESC(?score)

### RESULTS:
###
PREFIX  ### CHARSET LATIN1 ###
SELECT  DISTINCT ?cellType ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity ?efo_0000399_label ?expression ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?efo_0

            ?anatomical_entity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomical_entity_description.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene identifier and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_commonname ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_description ?taxon_scientificname ?gene_label ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_seealso ?gene_identifier

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY:
?anatomicalentity rdfs:label "APOC1" .
?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> "APOC1 is a member of the apoc1 gene family.  This gene is expressed in the post-juvenile stage.  See also http://www.uniprot.org/uniprot/P00

What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType      )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?stage ?gene

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY | ANATOMICALENTITY_NAME | SCORE | EFO_0005135 | STAGE | GENE | TAXON | SCIENTIFICNAME | ANATOMICALENTITY_DESCRIPTION
### GO:0005575       | ?               | ?      | ?          | ?     | ?     | human | ?          | ?
### NOTE:
### Check "Anatomical entities including cell types, if any" box.

###
### See also:
### http://purl.org/net/orth#GO_0005575
### http://purl.org/genex#expression_condition
### http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel
### http://purl.org/genex#hasSequenceUnit
### http://purl.org/net/orth#Gene
### http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName
### http://purl.org/dc/terms/description
###

###
### Anatomical entities including cell types, if any:
###   http://purl.org/net/orth#GO_0005575
###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity. # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	### Specifying species:
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:scientificName "Homo sapiens" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575        )
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity != ?anatomicalentity        )
    }

### EXPLANATION:

### AUTHOR:
<NAME>

### RELATION:

### DESCRIPTION:

Defines that the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed in the anatomical entity.

### See also:
http://purl.org/net/orth#isExpressedIn

### NOTE:
This example shows a gene expression relation.

### GENEX:AnatomicalEntity is a subclass of obo:GO_0005575.

### ORTH:Gene is a subclass of rdfs:Class.

### See also:
http://purl.org/net/orth#Gene

### ORTH:organism is a obo:RO_0002162.

### See also:
http://purl.org/ro/0002162

### FILE:
[gene_expression_relation.nt](http://purl.uniprot.org/core/gene_expression_relation.nt)

### See also:
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/gene_expression_relation.nt

### LANGUAGE:
N3

PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>

PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>

	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity. # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	### Specifying species:
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?anatName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?anat ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?efo_0000399_description ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex ?efo_0005135 . # has sex
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "male" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
}
ORDER BY ?anatName ?anat ?taxon ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?taxon_scientificname ?taxon_commonname ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description

43:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity. # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	### Specifying species:
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:scientificName "Homo sapiens" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575            )
    }

### EXPLANATION:
The following SPARQL query returns the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed.
The anatomical entity is a class, the anatomical entity name is the anatomical entity label.
The anatomical entity description is the anatomical entity description.
The gene is a gene, the gene see also is a gene see also, the gene description is a gene description.
Filtering by anatomical entity shows the anatomical entity where the gene is expressed.
Filtering by anatomical entity name shows the anatomical entity name where the gene is expressed.
Filtering by taxon shows the taxon where the gene is expressed.
Filtering by taxon scientific name shows the taxon scientific name where the gene is expressed.
Filtering by taxon common name shows the taxon common name where the gene is expressed.

### FILTER:
Check the checkboxes below to filter the result:
### CONTEXT:
    ?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentityName .
    ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description .
    ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/seeAlso> ?gene_seealso .
    ?organism <http://purl.org/ro/core#scientificName> ?taxon .

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:式
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135_label . # has strain
	?efo_0005135_label a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135_label rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?anatomicalentity . # in anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_seealso

    ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/label> "APOC1".

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0005135_label ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stage ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0005135 ?gene_description ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002155  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}

"APOC1"	"The human APOC1

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stageIRI ?anatName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?anat ?expression ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene dcterms:identifier "118230125" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stageIRI . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(          ?anat !=  obo:GO_0005575          )
}
ORDER BY ?anat ?score ?anatName

54:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene expression has expression level score.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType      )
}
ORDER BY desc(?score)

### RESULTS:

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the gene expression has expression level score.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
    PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
    PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0005135 ?score ?expression ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575    )
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType    )
}

### DESCRIPTION:
This query returns the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex. Provide also the gene expression has expression level score.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the gene expression has expression level score.

### SPARQL:POSEIDON?

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stageIRI ?anatName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?anat ?expression ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene dcterms:identifier "118230125" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stageIRI . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	FILTER(      ?anat !=  obo:GO_0005575      )
}

### DISCUSSION:
This query requires the genex:Expression and the genex:ExpressionCondition classes.
The eel gene apoc1 is expressed in all cell types, the developmental stage is independent of the strain, sex, and anatomical entity.
The expression has an expression level score, the strain <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> is labeled, and the gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> has the value <http://purl.org/dc/terms/118230125>.

### EXAMPLE:
Previous example.

58:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?taxon_commonname ?anatName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?anat ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex ?efo_0005135 . # has sex
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "male" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
} ORDER BY ?anatName ?anat ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description

### RESULT:

http://purl.uniprot.org/core/wild-type  ?anat ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier ?efo

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_label ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? ### SPARQL: ###

	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .

	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575            )
	FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType            )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?expression ?efo_0000399 ?gene

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>

	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?expressioncondition_strain . # has strain
	?expressioncondition_strain a genex:Strain.
	?expressioncondition_strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .

	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_description

76:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene label.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType      )
}
ORDER BY DESC(?score)

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_label ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier

### INSTRUCTION
