### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL: SHALL BE A STRING.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity . # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
}

Provides the anatomical entity where the APOC1 gene is expressed.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the P02654 gene is expressed? Note that P02654 is a UniProtKB identifier of the APOC1 human gene. Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity . # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
}

### RESULTS:
?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/label> ?anatomicalentityName.

### DESCRIPTION:
Anatomical entity is a class of the AnatomicalEntity label. Anatomical entity has description "An anatomical entity is a physical entity that can be identified using anatomical descriptions. Anatomical entities can be gene products or cell types or other types of biological entities. See also http://purl.org/dc/terms/label". Gene has see also <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> "APOC1 is a gene. APOC1 provides an important developmental function in the mammary gland. Mammary gland development requires the expression of APOC1 in luminal epithelial cells. See also http://purl.org/dc/terms/description".

### DESCRIPTOR:
http://purl.org/dc/terms/label
http://purl.org/dc/terms/description
http://purl.org/dc/terms/seeAlso
http://purl.org/dc/terms/description
http://purl.org/dc/terms/label

### EXAMPLE:
?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/label> ?anatomicalentityName.

87:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity DESC ?anatomicalentityName DESC ?score DESC ?expressioncondition DESC ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399 ?gene ?gene_label

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY: ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity =  obo:GO_0005575 ?cellType                  
### ANATOMICALENTITY: obo:GO_0005575

89:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?strain ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?taxon_commonname ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain . # has strain
	?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
}

### DESCRIPTION:
Provides the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type. Provides also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene identifier.

### ORIGIN:
This query was generated by the AnatomicalEntities SPARQL query generator.

### DESCRIPTION:
The AnatomicalEntities SPARQL query generator is a tool that allows you to generate any SPARQL query of the anatomicalentities category.

### SOURCE:
https://sparql.anatomicalentities.org/sparql

### VERSION:
2.0.1

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the gene expression has expression level score.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
    PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
    PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?stage ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?expression a genex:Expression .
		?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
		?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
		?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
		?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
		?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
		?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
		?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
		?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
		?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
		?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
		?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
		?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
		?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
		?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
		?organism obo:RO_0002155  ?taxon . # in taxon
		?taxon a up:Taxon .
		?taxon up:commonName "human" .
		?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
		?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
		?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
		?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
		FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575            )
		FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType            )
	}

### DESCRIPTION:
This query returns the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex. Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the gene expression has expression level score.

Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:式
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?strain ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stage ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain . # has strain
	?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity DESC ?anatomicalentityName DESC ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?expression ?

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
    PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
    PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene lscr:xrefStrain <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/NC_0000120> .
	?gene <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/taxonId> ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon <http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname .
	?taxon <http://purl.org/dc/terms/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575            )
	FILTER(            ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType            )
}

### DESCRIPTION:
This query returns the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex. Provide also the taxon scientific name, the taxon common name, the strain label, the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### QUERY DESCRIPTION:
The query retrieves the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex. Provide also the taxon scientific name, the taxon common name, the strain label, the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE {

	?expression a genex:Expression .

	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit

	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002152  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_description WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                )
} ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_description

98:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                  )
	FILTER(                  ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                  )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity DESC ?anatomicalentityName DESC ?score DESC

### RESULTS:
### ANATOMICALENTITY ?ANATOMICALENTITY_NAME ?ANATOMICALENTITY ?CELLTYPE ?EFO_0000399 ?SCORe

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0005135_label ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stage ?gene_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene_description ?efo_0005135 ?gene ?gene_seealso ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .

	?organism obo:RO_0002155  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
